This is the master context document for PLAYER ONE. Paste this at the start of any new chat to get full context. === PLAYER ONE — COMPLETE ARCHITECTURE REFERENCE === Version: May 2026 | Status: Active Development ━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━ TECH STACK ━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━━

what improvemebts could br done

13 May
Looking at your PLAYER ONE architecture, here are the improvements worth considering:

Quick Wins (Low effort, high impact)

The gemini.js file still named after Gemini is a maintenance smell — rename to groq.js or llmClient.js before the codebase grows further
The "Add Quest from JARVIS" feature is listed as console.log only — that's a broken core loop worth closing immediately
Font inconsistency (Syne vs Inter) should be resolved with a global find-replace before it silently breaks designs
Architecture

14+ Zustand stores is getting heavy. Consider grouping related ones — sdeStore + examStore + aiTrackStore could live under a learningStore namespace
jarvisContext.js pulling from all Supabase tables on every JARVIS call is expensive. Add a lightweight cache with a 60-second TTL so repeated quick messages don't re-fetch everything
Direct Groq calls scattered across 5+ files means rate limiting is inconsistent. Centralizing all AI calls through gemini.js (or its rename) gives you one place to manage retries, rate limits, and model swaps
Product gaps

No offline/PWA support — for a daily-use app this is a real friction point
No data export — you're building a year+ of personal data with no backup story
The Pomodoro store has no integration with Quest completion — finishing a pomodoro session could auto-suggest marking a quest done
Wallet is in paise but there's no spending mechanic shown — the economy feels one-directional
Longer term

The health habits are boolean flags in a single row — this won't scale when you want to add new habits without a schema migration
AI_TRACK_DATA as a hardcoded constant in the store means roadmap updates require a code deploy; moving it to Supabase gives you live edits
What area do you want to go deeper on?

whatmore improvemebts ciuld be done

13 May
Looking deeper at the architecture, here's what stands out:

Data & Persistence

No optimistic updates anywhere — every action waits for Supabase round-trip before UI updates, making the app feel slow
No error boundaries around pages — one bad Supabase response can crash the whole app silently
daily_completions tracks by date string but there's no timezone handling — if you're up past midnight, quests could log to the wrong day
No soft deletes — deleted quests/logs are gone forever, no recovery
AI / JARVIS

JARVIS has no memory across sessions beyond what collectFullContext() pulls — it can't recall "last Tuesday you mentioned feeling burnt out"
No streaming responses — JARVIS replies appear all at once after a delay; streaming would make it feel alive
Quest clusters are generated but if Groq is down, there's no fallback pool of pre-written quests
The evening debrief data (ratings, notes) isn't being used to influence future morning briefs — it's written but never read back
UX / Product

No notifications or reminders — the app is entirely pull-based, you have to remember to open it
Streak system has no grace period — miss one day and it resets; a "streak shield" mechanic would reduce frustration
No weekly review page — you log everything but there's no Sunday summary of what you actually accomplished
The XP formula sqrt(xp/100)+1 means early levels fly by and later ones slow down dramatically — worth testing if that feels motivating or discouraging around level 15+
No search across the app — finding a specific brain log or trade note requires navigating manually
Health specifically

Physique measurements have no visualization — raw numbers in a table tell you less than a simple line chart over 8 weeks
The ₹4/habit earning has no upper bound shown — does a perfect week display a satisfying total anywhere?
AI Coach sessions are stored but there's no way to compare advice from week 1 vs week 8
Trading

No win rate / expectancy calculation shown — the most important trading metric isn't surfaced
Trade journal entries are freeform text with no tagging — searching "all XAUUSD trades where I broke rules" isn't possible
No calendar view of trading days — hard to spot patterns like "I always lose on Mondays"
Developer experience

No TypeScript — with 14+ stores and complex data shapes, prop/state bugs are invisible until runtime
No tests anywhere — the XP engine and quest completion logic are critical paths with zero coverage
sdeSeeder.js and tradingSeeder.js as separate files suggests the seeding story is manual and fragile
The biggest missing piece — there's no "reflection loop." You're generating data (logs, trades, XP, brain drops) but nothing is analyzing it back at you. A weekly JARVIS digest that says "you completed 73% of quests, your trading win rate dropped, you skipped gym 3 times — here's what the pattern suggests" would make the whole system significantly more valuable.

Want me to sketch out how any of these would be implemented?

are ther more improvemts or this many

13 May
Honestly, that's a solid comprehensive list already. But there are a few more layers worth mentioning:

Security gaps (often overlooked)

Groq API key is VITE_ prefixed — meaning it's exposed in the browser bundle, visible to anyone who opens DevTools. Anyone can steal your API key and burn your credits
Supabase anon key is also client-side with no Row Level Security mentioned — if RLS isn't configured, anyone with your Supabase URL can read/write your personal data
No input sanitization on brain logs, trade notes, quest titles — potential XSS if any of it renders as HTML
Performance

Promise.all loading all 10+ stores on boot is aggressive — app probably has a noticeable loading delay every open
No pagination anywhere — after 6 months, brain_logs, trades, xp_log tables will have hundreds of rows being fetched entirely every time
Images/assets likely not optimized — Vite does some of this but no explicit lazy loading strategy mentioned
Mobile experience

BottomNav.jsx exists but the sidebar is 260px fixed — on small screens this probably fights for space
No haptic feedback on quest completion — small thing but makes mobile feel much more satisfying
Pomodoro has no background timer — if you switch tabs or lock phone, timer probably drifts or stops
Missing domains entirely

No sleep tracking beyond a boolean — you log "slept or didn't" but no hours, quality, bed/wake time
No social layer — nobody can see your progress, no accountability partner feature
No calendar integration — your exam dates, gym start date (June 16) live only in the app, not your actual calendar
No habit streaks per individual habit — only a global streak, so you can't tell which specific habit you keep breaking
Content / motivation design

Badges exist in the schema but no badge discovery UI — you don't know what badges exist to work toward
No "boss battles" — the getBossStatus() function exists in questEngine but nothing surfaces it in the UI
Level ups happen but there's no milestone meaning — level 10 feels the same as level 11, no unlocks, no narrative
No "prestige" system for when you complete the 14-month AI track — what happens after?
So to directly answer your question — you're probably at 85-90% of meaningful improvements now. The remaining 10-15% would be edge cases, polish, and features that only make sense after you've used the app daily for 3+ months and know what you actually need.

The highest ROI items across everything discussed are probably:

Fix the Groq API key exposure
Streaming JARVIS responses
The weekly reflection digest
Physique measurement charts
Trading win rate calculation
Want to start building any of these?

Here are your 4 prompts:

PROMPT 1 — Fixes #1, #4, #6, #7, #9
MISSION: Fix Groq API exposure, rename gemini.js, centralize all

=== FIX 1: Groq API Key Exposure ===

Open vite.config.js.
Add a proxy so the Groq key never reaches the browser bundle:

server: {
  proxy: {
    '/api/groq': {
      target: 'https://api.groq.com',
      changeOrigin: true,
      rewrite: (path) => path.replace(/^\/api\/groq/, ''),
      headers: {
        'Authorization': `Bearer ${process.env.VITE_GROQ_API_KEY}`
      }
    }
  }
}

All Groq fetch calls will now use '/api/groq/openai/v1/chat/completions'
instead of the full Groq URL. Fix this in groq.js (after rename in Fix 4).

=== FIX 6: Centralize All Groq Calls ===

Currently these files make direct Groq fetch calls bypassing groq.js:

In groq.js, add a new export alongside generateText:

export async function callGroq({ messages, max_tokens = 1000, 
temperature = 0.7, systemPrompt = null }) {
  if (systemPrompt) {
    messages = [{ role: 'system', content: systemPrompt }, ...messages]
  }
  try {
    const res = await fetch('/api/groq/openai/v1/chat/completions', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model: 'llama-3.3-70b-versatile',
        messages,
        max_tokens,
        temperature
      })
    })
    const data = await res.json()
    return { 
      text: data.choices?.[0]?.message?.content || '', 
      error: null 
    }
  } catch (err) {
    return { text: '', error: err.message }
  }
}

In each of the 5 files listed above:
Replace their inline fetch blocks with:
import { callGroq } from '../lib/groq'
const result = await callGroq({ messages: [...], max_tokens: 1000 })
const text = result.text

Do not change any logic around the calls — only replace the fetch block.

=== FIX 7: Error Boundaries on All 14 Pages ===

Create src/components/ErrorBoundary.jsx:

import { Component } from 'react'

export default class ErrorBoundary extends Component {
  constructor(props) {
    super(props)
    this.state = { hasError: false, error: null }
  }
  
  static getDerivedStateFromError(error) {
    return { hasError: true, error }
  }

  componentDidCatch(error, info) {
    console.error('Page error:', error, info)
  }

  render() {
    if (this.state.hasError) {
      return (
        <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center 
          h-full py-24 px-6">
          <div className="w-12 h-12 bg-[#C0392B]/10 rounded-2xl 
            flex items-center justify-center mb-4">
            <span className="text-[#C0392B] text-xl">!</span>
          </div>
          <p className="text-sm font-bold text-[#1A1A2E] 
            font-['Inter'] mb-1">
            Something went wrong
          </p>
          <p className="text-xs text-[#9A9590] font-['Inter'] 
            text-center mb-4 max-w-xs">
            {this.state.error?.message || 'An unexpected error occurred'}
          </p>
          <button
            onClick={() => this.setState({ hasError: false, error: null })}
            className="bg-[#1A1A2E] text-white px-4 py-2 rounded-xl
              text-xs font-bold font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase 
              tracking-wider"
          >
            Retry
          </button>
        </div>
      )
    }
    return this.props.children
  }
}

In App.jsx, wrap every lazy-loaded route:

Each route becomes:

    <CommandCenter />
  </ErrorBoundary>

=== FIX 9: JARVIS Streaming Responses ===

In src/store/jarvisStore.js, find the sendMessage action.
Replace the single fetch call with a streaming fetch:

const sendMessage = async (userMessage) => {
  // Add user message immediately
  const userMsg = { role: 'user', content: userMessage, 
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString() }
  set(state => ({ 
    chatHistory: [...state.chatHistory, userMsg],
    isStreaming: true,
    streamingContent: ''
  }))

  try {
    const context = await collectFullContext()
    const systemPrompt = buildSystemPrompt(context)
    
    const res = await fetch('/api/groq/openai/v1/chat/completions', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({
        model: 'llama-3.3-70b-versatile',
        messages: [
          { role: 'system', content: systemPrompt },
          ...get().chatHistory.map(m => ({ 
            role: m.role, content: m.content 
          }))
        ],
        max_tokens: 1000,
        stream: true
      })
    })

    const reader = res.body.getReader()
    const decoder = new TextDecoder()
    let fullContent = ''

    while (true) {
      const { done, value } = await reader.read()
      if (done) break
      
      const chunk = decoder.decode(value)
      const lines = chunk.split('\n').filter(l => l.startsWith('data: '))
      
      for (const line of lines) {
        const data = line.replace('data: ', '')
        if (data === '[DONE]') break
        try {
          const parsed = JSON.parse(data)
          const token = parsed.choices?.[0]?.delta?.content || ''
          fullContent += token
          set({ streamingContent: fullContent })
        } catch {}
      }
    }

    const assistantMsg = { 
      role: 'assistant', 
      content: fullContent,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    }
    set(state => ({
      chatHistory: [...state.chatHistory, assistantMsg],
      isStreaming: false,
      streamingContent: ''
    }))

  } catch (err) {
    console.error('JARVIS stream error:', err)
    set({ isStreaming: false, streamingContent: '' })
  }
}

Add to jarvisStore initial state:
isStreaming: false,
streamingContent: ''

In AIPlanner.jsx (JARVIS chat panel), find where assistant messages render.
If isStreaming is true, show a streaming bubble at the bottom:

{isStreaming && streamingContent && (
  <div className="flex gap-3">
    <div className="w-7 h-7 bg-[#1A1A2E] rounded-lg 
      flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
      <span className="text-white text-[10px]">J</span>
    </div>
    <div className="bg-white border border-[#E5E0D8] rounded-2xl 
      rounded-tl-sm px-4 py-3 max-w-[85%]">
      <p className="text-sm text-[#1A1A2E] font-['Inter'] 
        leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-wrap">
        {streamingContent}
        <span className="inline-block w-1 h-4 bg-[#E07B39] 
          ml-0.5 animate-pulse"/>
      </p>
    </div>
  </div>
)}

=== FIX 13: Weekly Reflection Digest ===

In CommandCenter.jsx, add a new card below the morning greeting card.

Add state:
const [digest, setDigest] = useState(null)
const [isGeneratingDigest, setIsGeneratingDigest] = useState(false)
const [digestExpanded, setDigestExpanded] = useState(false)

Add generator function:
const generateWeeklyDigest = async () => {
  setIsGeneratingDigest(true)
  try {
    const { callGroq } = await import('../lib/groq')
    
    // Fetch this week's data
    const weekStart = new Date()
    weekStart.setDate(weekStart.getDate() - weekStart.getDay())
    const weekStartStr = weekStart.toISOString().split('T')[0]
    
    const [questRes, healthRes, xpRes] = await Promise.all([
      supabase.from('daily_completions')
        .select('*').gte('completed_date', weekStartStr),
      supabase.from('health_logs')
        .select('*').gte('log_date', weekStartStr),
      supabase.from('xp_log')
        .select('*').gte('created_at', weekStartStr)
    ])

    const totalXP = xpRes.data?.reduce((s, r) => s + r.amount, 0) || 0
    const questsDone = questRes.data?.length || 0
    const healthDays = healthRes.data?.length || 0
    const avgScore = healthRes.data?.length 
      ? Math.round(healthRes.data.reduce((s,r) => 
          s + (r.day_score || 0), 0) / healthRes.data.length)
      : 0

    const result = await callGroq({
      messages: [{
        role: 'user',
        content: `Abhishek's week in numbers:
        - Quests completed: ${questsDone}
        - XP earned: ${totalXP}
        - Health days logged: ${healthDays}/7
        - Average health score: ${avgScore}%
        
        Write a 3-sentence weekly reflection. 
        Sentence 1: What the numbers say about this week.
        Sentence 2: One specific thing to fix next week.
        Sentence 3: One thing to be proud of.
        Be direct. No fluff. Max 80 words.`
      }],
      max_tokens: 200,
      temperature: 0.7
    })

    setDigest({
      text: result.text,
      questsDone,
      totalXP,
      healthDays,
      avgScore,
      generatedAt: new Date().toISOString()
    })
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('digest error:', err)
  }
  setIsGeneratingDigest(false)
}

Add digest card JSX (below morning brief, above stats row):

        Weekly Digest
      </p>
      <p className="text-sm font-bold text-[#1A1A2E] font-['Inter']">
        This Week So Far
      </p>
    </div>
    <button
      onClick={() => setDigestExpanded(!digestExpanded)}
      className="text-xs text-[#9A9590] font-['Space_Mono'] 
        uppercase tracking-wider"
    >
      {digestExpanded ? 'Hide' : 'Show'}
    </button>
  </div>

  {/* Stats row always visible */}
  <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-3 mb-3">
    {[
      { label: 'Quests', value: digest?.questsDone ?? '—' },
      { label: 'XP', value: digest?.totalXP ?? '—' },
      { label: 'Health Days', value: digest ? `${digest.healthDays}/7` : '—' },
      { label: 'Avg Score', value: digest ? `${digest.avgScore}%` : '—' }
    ].map(stat => (
      <div key={stat.label} className="bg-[#F5F4F0] rounded-xl p-3 
        text-center">
        <p className="text-base font-bold text-[#1A1A2E]

    ))}
  </div>

  {digestExpanded && (
    <div>
      {!digest && !isGeneratingDigest && (
        <button

          className="w-full bg-[#1A1A2E] text-white py-2.5 rounded-xl

      )}

        <div className="bg-[#F5F4F0] rounded-xl p-4 
          border-l-4 border-[#E07B39]">
          <p className="text-sm text-[#1A1A2E] font-['Inter'] 
            leading-relaxed">{digest.text}</p>
          <button onClick={generateWeeklyDigest}
            className="text-[9px] text-[#9A9590] font-['Space_Mono'] 
              uppercase tracking-wider mt-3 hover:text-[#E07B39]
              transition-colors">
            Refresh
          </button>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  )}
</div>

export const LEVEL_MILESTONES = {

    description: 'JARVIS now pulls 90 days of context instead of 30.',
    color: '#C0392B',
    icon: '🏆'
  }
}

export function getMilestoneForLevel(level) {
  return LEVEL_MILESTONES[level] || null
}

export function getNextMilestone(level) {
  const milestonelevels = Object.keys(LEVEL_MILESTONES).map(Number)
  const next = milestonelevels.find(l => l > level)
  return next ? { level: next, ...LEVEL_MILESTONES[next] } : null
}

  const from = brainLogsPage * 20
  const to = from + 19

    .from('brain_logs')

      brainLogsPage: brainLogsPage + 1,
      brainLogsHasMore: data.length === 20
    }))
  }
}

=== FIX 28: Optimistic UI Updates ===

Apply optimistic updates to 3 high-frequency actions:

1. completeDaily in questStore.js:
Before the Supabase insert:
// Optimistic: add to todayCompletions immediately
set(state => ({
  todayCompletions: [...state.todayCompletions, questId]
}))

// Then do Supabase insert
const { error } = await supabase.from('daily_completions').insert(...)

// If error, rollback
if (error) {
  set(state => ({
    todayCompletions: state.todayCompletions.filter(id => id !== questId)
  }))
  return
}

2. updateLog in healthStore.js (habit checkbox toggle):
Before Supabase upsert:
// Optimistic: update todayLog immediately
set(state => ({
  todayLog: { ...state.todayLog, [field]: value }
}))

// Then Supabase upsert
const { error } = await supabase.from('health_logs').upsert(...)

// If error, rollback
if (error) {
  set(state => ({
    todayLog: { ...state.todayLog, [field]: !value }
  }))
}

3. togglePhase1 / togglePhase2 in aiTrackStore.js:
Before Supabase upsert:
// Optimistic
set(state => ({
  progress: {
    ...state.progress,
    [topicId]: {
      ...state.progress[topicId],
      phase1_done: !state.progress[topicId]?.phase1_done
    }
  }
}))

// Then Supabase
const { error } = await supabase.from('ai_track_progress').upsert(...)

// If error, rollback by re-toggling
if (error) {
  set(state => ({
    progress: {
      ...state.progress,
      [topicId]: {
        ...state.progress[topicId],
        phase1_done: !state.progress[topicId]?.phase1_done
      }
    }
  }))
}

=== FIX 29: Pomodoro Background Timer ===

In src/store/pomodoroStore.js, replace the setInterval approach
with a timestamp-based approach:

Add to store state:
startedAt: null,
expectedEndAt: null

When startTimer is called:
const now = Date.now()
const durationMs = get().currentDuration * 60 * 1000
set({
  isRunning: true,
  startedAt: now,
  expectedEndAt: now + durationMs
})

Replace the tick interval with a visibility-aware approach.
In Pomodoro.jsx:

useEffect(() => {
  let interval = null
  
  const tick = () => {
    const { isRunning, expectedEndAt } = usePomodoroStore.getState()
    if (!isRunning || !expectedEndAt) return
    
    const remaining = Math.max(0, expectedEndAt - Date.now())
    const minutes = Math.floor(remaining / 60000)
    const seconds = Math.floor((remaining % 60000) / 1000)
    
    setDisplayTime({ minutes, seconds })
    
    if (remaining <= 0) {
      usePomodoroStore.getState().skipPhase()
      clearInterval(interval)
    }
  }

  if (isRunning) {
    tick() // immediate
    interval = setInterval(tick, 1000)
  }

  // Recalculate on tab visibility change
  const onVisible = () => {
    if (document.visibilityState === 'visible') tick()
  }
  document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', onVisible)

  return () => {
    clearInterval(interval)
    document.removeEventListener('visibilitychange', onVisible)
  }
}, [isRunning])

Add local state to Pomodoro.jsx:
const [displayTime, setDisplayTime] = useState({ 
  minutes: 25, seconds: 0 
})

Replace all references to store minutes/seconds with 
displayTime.minutes and displayTime.seconds.

=== FIX 32: Soft Delete with Recovery ===

Add deleted_at column support (do not run migrations —
use a soft delete flag in the existing tables via a 
convention in the store).

In questStore.js, replace deleteDailyQuest:

deleteDailyQuest: async (questId) => {
  // Optimistic: remove from UI
  const deletedQuest = get().dailyQuests.find(q => q.id === questId)
  set(state => ({
    dailyQuests: state.dailyQuests.filter(q => q.id !== questId),
    recentlyDeleted: [...(state.recentlyDeleted || []), deletedQuest]
  }))

  // Show undo toast for 5 seconds before actual delete
  // The actual Supabase delete happens after 5s if not undone
  const deleteTimeout = setTimeout(async () => {
    await supabase.from('daily_quests').delete().eq('id', questId)
    set(state => ({
      recentlyDeleted: state.recentlyDeleted.filter(q => q.id !== questId)
    }))
  }, 5000)

  // Store timeout reference
  set(state => ({
    deleteTimeouts: { 
      ...(state.deleteTimeouts || {}), 
      [questId]: deleteTimeout 
    }
  }))
},

undoDelete: (questId) => {
  const { recentlyDeleted, deleteTimeouts } = get()
  
  // Cancel the timeout
  if (deleteTimeouts?.[questId]) {
    clearTimeout(deleteTimeouts[questId])
  }
  
  // Restore to UI
  const quest = recentlyDeleted?.find(q => q.id === questId)
  if (quest) {
    set(state => ({
      dailyQuests: [...state.dailyQuests, quest],
      recentlyDeleted: state.recentlyDeleted.filter(q => q.id !== questId),
      deleteTimeouts: Object.fromEntries(
        Object.entries(state.deleteTimeouts || {})
          .filter(([k]) => k !== questId)
      )
    }))
  }
},

Add to questStore initial state:
recentlyDeleted: [],
deleteTimeouts: {}

In QuestLog.jsx, after quest delete:
triggerJarvisToast({
  type: 'warning',
  title: 'Quest Deleted',
  message: 'Tap to undo',
  duration: 5000,
  onAction: () => undoDelete(questId)
})

Add onAction support to JarvisToast.jsx if not present:
In the toast render, if toast.onAction exists:
<button onClick={toast.onAction} 
  className="text-[9px] font-bold text-white/80 
    font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-wider 
    underline mt-1">
  Undo
</button>

=== FIX 33: Data Export ===

In src/pages/Settings.jsx, find the danger zone section.
Above it, add an Export Data section.

Add export handler:
const exportAllData = async () => {
  setIsExporting(true)
  try {
    const tables = [
      'player_state', 'xp_log', 'daily_quests', 
      'daily_completions', 'health_logs', 'physique_logs',
      'brain_logs', 'trades', 'trade_journal',
      'explorer_topics', 'brain_drops', 'ai_track_progress',
      'ai_sessions', 'books', 'income_milestones'
    ]

    const exportData = {}
    
    await Promise.all(tables.map(async (table) => {
      const { data } = await supabase.from(table).select('*')
      exportData[table] = data || []
    }))

    exportData._exported_at = new Date().toISOString()
    exportData._version = '1.0'

    const blob = new Blob(
      [JSON.stringify(exportData, null, 2)], 
      { type: 'application/json' }
    )
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob)
    const a = document.createElement('a')
    a.href = url
    a.download = `player-one-export-${
      new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]
    }.json`
    a.click()
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url)

    triggerJarvisToast({
      type: 'success',
      title: 'Export Complete',
      message: `${tables.length} tables exported successfully`,
      jarvisLine: 'Your data is yours. Always.'
    })
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('export error:', err)
    triggerJarvisToast({
      type: 'warning',
      title: 'Export Failed',
      message: err.message
    })
  }
  setIsExporting(false)
}

Add state: const [isExporting, setIsExporting] = useState(false)

Export section UI (above danger zone):
<div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-[#E5E0D8] p-5 mb-4">
  <p className="text-[10px] font-bold text-[#9A9590] 
    font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-widest mb-1">
    Data Export
  </p>
  <p className="text-sm font-bold text-[#1A1A2E] font-['Inter'] mb-1">
    Export All Your Data
  </p>
  <p className="text-xs text-[#9A9590] font-['Inter'] mb-4">
    Downloads a JSON file with all your progress, logs, 
    trades, and history. Keep this as a backup.
  </p>
  <button
    onClick={exportAllData}
    disabled={isExporting}
    className="bg-[#1A1A2E] text-white px-5 py-2.5 rounded-xl
      text-xs font-bold font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase 
      tracking-wider disabled:opacity-50 transition-all"
  >
    {isExporting ? 'Exporting...' : 'Export JSON'}
  </button>
</div>

=== FIX 35: Health Earnings Summary ===

In src/pages/Health.jsx, find the daily tab section.

Add earnings calculator:
const todayEarnings = useMemo(() => {
  if (!todayLog) return 0
  const habitFields = [
    'gym_done', 'steps_done', 'water_done', 'sleep_done',
    'no_junk', 'skincare_done', 'grooming_done', 
    'vitamins_done', 'reading_done', 'no_social_media'
  ]
  const checked = habitFields.filter(f => todayLog[f]).length
  return checked * 4
}, [todayLog])

const weekEarnings = useMemo(() => {
  return (healthHistory || [])
    .filter(log => {
      const logDate = new Date(log.log_date)
      const weekStart = new Date()
      weekStart.setDate(weekStart.getDate() - weekStart.getDay() + 1)
      weekStart.setHours(0,0,0,0)
      return logDate >= weekStart
    })
    .reduce((sum, log) => sum + (log.rupees_earned || 0), 0)
}, [healthHistory])

const perfectDaysThisWeek = useMemo(() => {
  return (healthHistory || [])
    .filter(log => {
      const logDate = new Date(log.log_date)
      const weekStart = new Date()
      weekStart.setDate(weekStart.getDate() - weekStart.getDay() + 1)
      weekStart.setHours(0,0,0,0)
      return logDate >= weekStart && log.day_score === 100
    }).length
}, [healthHistory])

        Today

    <div>
      <p className="text-xl font-bold text-white

Add Past Sessions section below the AI Coach prompt buttons:

<div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-[#E5E0D8] p-5 mt-4">
  <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
    <p className="text-[10px] font-bold text-[#9A9590] 
      font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-widest">
      Past Sessions
    </p>
    {sessions.length >= 2 && (
      <button
        onClick={() => setCompareMode(!compareMode)}
        className={`text-[9px] font-bold font-['Space_Mono'] 
          uppercase tracking-wider px-2.5 py-1 rounded-lg
          transition-all ${compareMode 
            ? 'bg-[#1A1A2E] text-white' 
            : 'bg-[#F5F4F0] text-[#9A9590]'}`}
      >
        {compareMode ? 'Cancel' : 'Compare'}
      </button>
    )}
  </div>

  {isLoadingSessions && (
    <div className="space-y-2">
      {[1,2,3].map(i => (
        <div key={i} className="h-12 bg-[#F5F4F0] rounded-xl 
          animate-pulse"/>
      ))}
    </div>
  )}

  {sessions.map(session => (
    <div
      key={session.id}
      onClick={() => {
        if (!compareMode) return
        setSelectedSessions(prev => 
          prev.includes(session.id)
            ? prev.filter(id => id !== session.id)
            : prev.length < 2 
              ? [...prev, session.id]
              : prev
        )
      }}
      className={`p-3 rounded-xl mb-2 cursor-pointer
        border transition-all
        ${compareMode && selectedSessions.includes(session.id)
          ? 'border-[#E07B39] bg-[#E07B39]/5'
          : 'border-[#E5E0D8] bg-[#F5F4F0] hover:border-[#1A1A2E]'
        }`}
    >
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <p className="text-xs font-bold text-[#1A1A2E] 
          font-['Inter']">
          {session.prompt_type?.replace('_', ' ')} 
          — {new Date(session.session_date)
            .toLocaleDateString('en-IN', { 
              day: 'numeric', month: 'short' 
            })}
        </p>
        {compareMode && selectedSessions.includes(session.id) && (
          <span className="text-[9px] font-bold text-[#E07B39] 
            font-['Space_Mono']">
            Selected
          </span>
        )}
      </div>
      <p className="text-[10px] text-[#9A9590] font-['Inter'] 
        mt-0.5 line-clamp-1">
        {session.ai_response?.substring(0, 80)}...
      </p>
    </div>
  ))}

  {compareMode && selectedSessions.length === 2 && (
    <div className="mt-4 grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
      {selectedSessions.map(id => {
        const s = sessions.find(s => s.id === id)
        return (
          <div key={id} className="bg-white rounded-xl 
            border border-[#E5E0D8] p-3">
            <p className="text-[9px] font-bold text-[#E07B39] 
              font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-wider mb-2">
              {new Date(s.session_date).toLocaleDateString('en-IN',
                { day: 'numeric', month: 'short' })}
            </p>
            <p className="text-xs text-[#1A1A2E] font-['Inter'] 
              leading-relaxed">
              {s.ai_response}
            </p>
          </div>
        )
      })}
    </div>
  )}
</div>

                rounded-xl text-xs font-bold font-['Space_Mono'] 
                uppercase tracking-wider hover:opacity-90">
              Generate Prestige Roadmap
            </button>
          </div>
        )}

        {isGeneratingPrestige && (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-3 py-8 
            justify-center">
            <div className="w-8 h-8 bg-[#7C3AED] rounded-xl 
              flex items-center justify-center animate-pulse">
              <Brain size={16} className="text-white"/>
            </div>
            <p className="text-sm text-[#9A9590] 
              font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-wider">
              Charting your next frontier...
            </p>
          </div>
        )}

        {prestigeResponse && (
          <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }}>
            <div className="bg-[#F5F4F0] rounded-xl p-5 
              border-l-4 border-[#7C3AED] mb-4">
              <p className="text-sm text-[#1A1A2E] font-['Inter'] 
                leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-wrap">
                {prestigeResponse}
              </p>
            </div>
            <button
              onClick={generatePrestigeRoadmap}
              disabled={isGeneratingPrestige}
              className="text-xs text-[#9A9590] font-['Space_Mono']

                transition-colors flex items-center gap-1"
            >
              <RefreshCw size={11}/> Regenerate
            </button>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </div>
    )}
  </motion.div>
)}

13 May
Here's exactly what it does in plain terms:

Change 1 — Prestige Response Persistence

When you open the AI Engineer Track page, it checks Supabase for any previously generated prestige roadmap
If one exists, it loads it automatically — so you don't see a blank "Generate Prestige Roadmap" button every time
When you generate or regenerate a prestige roadmap, it saves that response to Supabase
Next time you open the page, it's already there waiting
Change 2 — JARVIS Memory

Every time JARVIS responds to you (morning brief, chat, evening debrief, AI coach), it gets saved to ai_sessions table — this was already happening
Now when you open JARVIS, before it replies it first reads the last 20 saved sessions from that table
It passes those sessions into its system prompt so it knows what you talked about before
So instead of JARVIS starting fresh every conversation, it can say things like "last week you mentioned struggling with consistency" or "you already covered X topic"
What it does NOT do

Does not change any UI
Does not change any page layout
Does not add any new tables
Does not break anything existing
Only touches 3 files: AIEngineerTrack.jsx, jarvisContext.js, jarvisPrompt.js

AI Engineer Track approach:

You're following CampusX 14-month roadmap. The page has 3 clusters (A/B/C) each with sections and 150+ topics. Each topic has two phases:

Phase 1 — Week 1: explore the topic (orange compass toggle)
Phase 2 — Week 2: actually study it deep (cluster color check toggle)
Every week JARVIS generates a weekly goal for that week's topics with a Mon-Sun breakdown and a deliverable. When you mark a week complete it auto-generates the next week. Topics can expand to show a JARVIS-generated exploration (curiosity hook, key questions, concepts, books, papers) which saves to Supabase. Notes per topic auto-save.

Explorer approach:

Completely separate from AI Track. This is your intellectual curiosity system. Every week JARVIS picks a topic from Psychology, Neuroscience, Cognitive Science, Geopolitics, or AI. It generates 5 concepts that build on each other, 3 books, 3 papers, an ignition hook and a big question. You read concepts and mark them done, drop brain drops (quick thoughts), write research notes. Knowledge depth per domain tracks how deep you've gone. Archive stores all past weekly topics.

PROMPT 1 — Daily Intention Input
MISSION: Add daily intention input to morning brief flow.
Store it in Supabase. JARVIS references it in evening debrief.
Do not touch any existing morning brief or evening debrief logic.
Only add new intention layer on top.

=== CHANGE 1: Add intention column to ai_sessions ===

No migration needed. Store intention as a separate row type.
When saving intention, insert new row:
{
  type: 'daily_intention',
  session_date: getTodayIST(),
  user_input: intentionText,
  ai_response: '',
  context_snapshot: '{}'
}

=== CHANGE 2: Add intention state to jarvisStore.js ===

Add to initial state:
  todayIntention: '',
  intentionSaved: false,
  isLoadingIntention: false

Add loadTodayIntention action:
const loadTodayIntention = async () => {
  const today = getTodayIST()
  const { data } = await supabase
    .from('ai_sessions')
    .select('user_input')
    .eq('type', 'daily_intention')
    .eq('session_date', today)
    .single()
  if (data?.user_input) {
    set({ 
      todayIntention: data.user_input, 
      intentionSaved: true 
    })
  }
}

Add saveIntention action:
const saveIntention = async (text) => {
  if (!text.trim()) return
  const today = getTodayIST()
  
  // Check if already saved today
  const { data: existing } = await supabase
    .from('ai_sessions')
    .select('id')
    .eq('type', 'daily_intention')
    .eq('session_date', today)
    .single()

  if (existing) {
    await supabase
      .from('ai_sessions')
      .update({ user_input: text })
      .eq('id', existing.id)
  } else {
    await supabase
      .from('ai_sessions')
      .insert({
        type: 'daily_intention',
        session_date: today,
        user_input: text,
        ai_response: '',
        context_snapshot: '{}'
      })
  }
  set({ todayIntention: text, intentionSaved: true })
  triggerJarvisToast({
    type: 'success',
    title: 'Intention Set',
    message: text.substring(0, 50),
    jarvisLine: 'Locked in. Now execute.'
  })
}

Export: loadTodayIntention, saveIntention, todayIntention,
  intentionSaved from jarvisStore.

PROMPT 2 — Pre-Trade ICT/SMC Checklist

=== CHANGE 1: Create ICT checklist component ===

Create src/components/TradeChecklist.jsx:

import { useState } from 'react'
import { CheckCircle2, Circle, AlertTriangle } from 'lucide-react'

const ICT_RULES = [
  {
    id: 'htf_bias',
    rule: 'HTF Bias Confirmed',
    description: 'Higher timeframe structure supports your direction'
  },
  {
    id: 'displacement',
    rule: 'Displacement Present',
    description: 'Strong impulse move created the imbalance'
  },
  {
    id: 'poi_identified',
    rule: 'POI Clearly Identified',
    description: 'Order block or FVG is well-defined on LTF'
  },
  {
    id: 'kill_zone',
    rule: 'Kill Zone Entry',
    description: 'Entry during London, NY open or overlap session'
  },
  {
    id: 'liquidity_taken',
    rule: 'Liquidity Swept',
    description: 'Equal highs/lows or stop hunts confirmed before entry'
  },
  {
    id: 'risk_defined',
    rule: 'Risk Clearly Defined',
    description: 'Stop loss placed, position size calculated before entry'
  }
]

export default function TradeChecklist({ onComplete, onSkip }) {
  const [checked, setChecked] = useState({})
  
  const checkedCount = Object.values(checked).filter(Boolean).length
  const allChecked = checkedCount === ICT_RULES.length
  const passRate = Math.round((checkedCount / ICT_RULES.length) * 100)

  const toggle = (id) => {
    setChecked(prev => ({ ...prev, [id]: !prev[id] }))
  }

  return (
    <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-[#E5E0D8] p-5">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-4">
        <div>
          <p className="text-[10px] font-bold text-[#9A9590]
            font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-widest mb-0.5">
            Pre-Trade Checklist
          </p>
          <p className="text-sm font-bold text-[#1A1A2E] 
            font-['Inter']">
            ICT / SMC Rules
          </p>
        </div>
        <div className="text-right">
          <p className="text-2xl font-bold font-['Space_Mono']"
            style={{ color: passRate === 100 
              ? '#1A6B4A' 
              : passRate >= 66 
                ? '#E07B39' 
                : '#C0392B' }}>
            {checkedCount}/{ICT_RULES.length}
          </p>
          <p className="text-[9px] text-[#9A9590] 
            font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-wider">
            Rules Met
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div className="space-y-2 mb-4">
        {ICT_RULES.map(rule => (
          <button
            key={rule.id}
            onClick={() => toggle(rule.id)}
            className={`w-full flex items-start gap-3 p-3 
              rounded-xl text-left transition-all border
              ${checked[rule.id]
                ? 'bg-[#1A6B4A]/5 border-[#1A6B4A]/30'
                : 'bg-[#F5F4F0] border-transparent'}`}
          >
            {checked[rule.id]
              ? <CheckCircle2 size={16} 
                  className="text-[#1A6B4A] shrink-0 mt-0.5"/>
              : <Circle size={16} 
                  className="text-[#9A9590] shrink-0 mt-0.5"/>
            }
            <div>
              <p className={`text-xs font-bold font-['Inter']
                ${checked[rule.id] 
                  ? 'text-[#1A6B4A]' 
                  : 'text-[#1A1A2E]'}`}>
                {rule.rule}
              </p>
              <p className="text-[10px] text-[#9A9590] 
                font-['Inter'] mt-0.5">
                {rule.description}
              </p>
            </div>
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      {checkedCount < 4 && (
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 bg-[#C0392B]/5 
          rounded-xl p-3 mb-4 border border-[#C0392B]/20">
          <AlertTriangle size={14} className="text-[#C0392B] shrink-0"/>
          <p className="text-xs text-[#C0392B] font-['Inter']">
            Less than 4 rules met. Are you sure this is a 
            valid setup?
          </p>
        </div>
      )}

      <div className="flex gap-2">
        <button
          onClick={() => onComplete({ 
            checklist: checked, 
            rulesScore: passRate 
          })}
          className={`flex-1 py-2.5 rounded-xl text-xs font-bold
            font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-wider
            transition-all text-white
            ${allChecked 
              ? 'bg-[#1A6B4A]' 
              : checkedCount >= 4 
                ? 'bg-[#E07B39]' 
                : 'bg-[#1A1A2E]'}`}
        >
          {allChecked 
            ? 'Perfect Setup — Log Trade' 
            : checkedCount >= 4 
              ? 'Acceptable Setup — Continue'
              : 'Proceed Anyway'}
        </button>
        <button
          onClick={onSkip}
          className="px-4 py-2.5 rounded-xl text-xs font-bold
            font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-wider
            bg-[#F5F4F0] text-[#9A9590] hover:text-[#1A1A2E]
            transition-colors"
        >
          Skip
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  )
}

PROMPT 3 — Pattern Alerts in JARVIS
MISSION: Add automatic pattern detection to JARVIS.
JARVIS analyzes existing Supabase data and surfaces behavioral
patterns without user asking. New file only + small addition
to CommandCenter. Zero changes to existing JARVIS chat or stores.

=== CHANGE 1: Create src/lib/patternDetector.js ===

export async function detectPatterns(supabase) {
  const patterns = []
  const today = new Date()
  
  // Fetch last 14 days of data
  const fourteenDaysAgo = new Date()
  fourteenDaysAgo.setDate(fourteenDaysAgo.getDate() - 14)
  const fromDate = fourteenDaysAgo.toISOString().split('T')[0]

  const [healthRes, questRes, tradeRes] = await Promise.all([
    supabase.from('health_logs')
      .select('log_date, gym_done, day_score, rupees_earned')
      .gte('log_date', fromDate)
      .order('log_date', { ascending: true }),
    supabase.from('daily_completions')
      .select('completed_date, quest_id')
      .gte('completed_date', fromDate),
    supabase.from('trades')
      .select('date, pnl, rules_followed')
      .gte('date', fromDate)
      .order('date', { ascending: true })
  ])

  const healthLogs = healthRes.data || []
  const completions = questRes.data || []
  const trades = tradeRes.data || []

  // PATTERN 1: Gym skip streak
  const lastNDays = (n) => {
    const days = []
    for (let i = n - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
      const d = new Date()
      d.setDate(d.getDate() - i)
      days.push(d.toISOString().split('T')[0])
    }
    return days
  }

  const last3Days = lastNDays(3)
  const gymSkips = last3Days.filter(date => {
    const log = healthLogs.find(l => l.log_date === date)
    return log && !log.gym_done
  })
  if (gymSkips.length === 3) {
    patterns.push({
      type: 'warning',
      icon: '💪',
      title: 'Gym Skip Streak',
      message: 'You have skipped gym 3 days in a row.',
      action: 'Break the pattern today.'
    })
  }

  // PATTERN 2: Monday quest drop
  const mondayCompletions = completions.filter(c => {
    const day = new Date(c.completed_date).getDay()
    return day === 1
  })
  const otherCompletions = completions.filter(c => {
    const day = new Date(c.completed_date).getDay()
    return day !== 1 && day !== 0
  })
  const mondayAvg = mondayCompletions.length / 2
  const otherAvg = otherCompletions.length / 8
  if (otherAvg > 0 && mondayAvg < otherAvg * 0.5) {
    patterns.push({
      type: 'info',
      icon: '📅',
      title: 'Monday Dip Detected',
      message: 'Your quest completion is significantly lower on Mondays.',
      action: 'Prep Sunday night for a strong Monday.'
    })
  }

  // PATTERN 3: Consecutive losses
  const last5Trades = trades.slice(-5)
  const consecutiveLosses = last5Trades
    .filter(t => parseFloat(t.pnl) < 0).length
  if (consecutiveLosses >= 3 && last5Trades.length >= 3) {
    patterns.push({
      type: 'danger',
      icon: '⚠️',
      title: 'Drawdown Alert',
      message: `${consecutiveLosses} of your last 5 trades were losses.`,
      action: 'Step back. Review HTF bias before next trade.'
    })
  }

  // PATTERN 4: High score streak
  const last7Days = lastNDays(7)
  const highScoreDays = last7Days.filter(date => {
    const log = healthLogs.find(l => l.log_date === date)
    return log && log.day_score >= 80
  })
  if (highScoreDays.length >= 5) {
    patterns.push({
      type: 'success',
      icon: '🔥',
      title: 'On Fire',
      message: `${highScoreDays.length} high-score health days this week.`,
      action: 'Keep this momentum going.'
    })
  }

  // PATTERN 5: No quests for X days
  const todayStr = today.toISOString().split('T')[0]
  const last3DaysQuests = lastNDays(3).filter(date => 
    date !== todayStr
  )
  const questGap = last3DaysQuests.filter(date =>
    !completions.find(c => c.completed_date === date)
  )
  if (questGap.length === 2) {
    patterns.push({
      type: 'warning',
      icon: '📋',
      title: 'Quest Gap',
      message: 'No quests completed in the last 2 days.',
      action: 'Open Quest Log and approve a cluster now.'
    })
  }

  // PATTERN 6: No SDE domain quests
  const { data: sdeCompletions } = await supabase
    .from('daily_completions')
    .select('quest_id, daily_quests(domain)')
    .gte('completed_date', fromDate)
  
  const sdeDone = (sdeCompletions || []).filter(c => 
    c.daily_quests?.domain === 'sde'
  )
  if (sdeDone.length === 0 && completions.length > 10) {
    patterns.push({
      type: 'info',
      icon: '💻',
      title: 'SDE Neglect',
      message: 'No SDE quests completed in 14 days.',
      action: 'Generate a coding cluster today.'
    })
  }

  return patterns
}

      ))}

  </div>
)}

MISSION: Add difficulty rating to AI Track topics after phase2

=== CHANGE 2: Add rating actions to aiTrackStore.js ===

Add to initial state:
  difficultyRatings: {}

In loadProgress action, after fetching ai_track_progress rows,
extract difficulty ratings:
const ratings = {}
data.forEach(row => {
  if (row.difficulty_rating !== null && 
      row.difficulty_rating !== undefined) {
    ratings[row.topic_id] = row.difficulty_rating
  }
})
set(state => ({ 
  ...state, 
  progress: progressMap,
  difficultyRatings: ratings 
}))

Add rateTopic action:
rateTopic: async (topicId, topicTitle, sectionId, cluster, rating) => {
  set(state => ({
    difficultyRatings: { 
      ...state.difficultyRatings, 
      [topicId]: rating 
    }
  }))
  
  await supabase
    .from('ai_track_progress')
    .upsert({
      topic_id: topicId,
      topic_title: topicTitle,
      section_id: sectionId,
      cluster: cluster,
      difficulty_rating: rating,
      updated_at: new Date().toISOString()
    }, { onConflict: 'topic_id' })
},

Add computed getter getRevisionQueue:
getRevisionQueue: () => {
  const { difficultyRatings, progress } = get()
  return Object.entries(difficultyRatings)
    .filter(([topicId, rating]) => 
      rating >= 4 && progress[topicId]?.phase2_done
    )
    .map(([topicId, rating]) => ({ topicId, rating }))
    .sort((a, b) => b.rating - a.rating)
},

Export: rateTopic, difficultyRatings, getRevisionQueue

      How Hard Was This?
    </p>

      {[1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map(star => (
        <button

            star

              : 'bg-[#F5F4F0] text-[#9A9590] border-[#E5E0D8]'
            }`}

          {star}
        </button>
      ))}
      {difficultyRatings[topic.id] && (

          AI_TRACK_DATA.clusters.forEach(c => {

                  ...t, 
                  sectionTitle: s.title,
                  clusterName: c.name 
                }
              })
            })
          })
          if (!topicData) return null
          return (
            <div key={topicId}
              className="bg-white rounded-2xl border 
                border-[#E5E0D8] p-4">
              <div className="flex items-start 
                justify-between gap-3">
                <div className="flex-1">

                    text-[#9A9590] font-['Space_Mono'] 
                    uppercase tracking-wider mb-0.5">
                    {topicData.clusterName} → {topicData.sectionTitle}
                  </p>
                  <p className="text-sm font-bold text-[#1A1A2E]
                    font-['Inter']">
                    {topicData.title}
                  </p>
                </div>
                <div className="flex gap-0.5 shrink-0">
                  {[1,2,3,4,5].map(s => (
                    <div key={s}
                      className={`w-3 h-3 rounded-sm
                        ${s <= rating 
                          ? 'bg-[#C0392B]' 
                          : 'bg-[#E5E0D8]'}`}
                    />
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          )
        })}
      </div>
    )}
  </div>
)}

=== CHANGE 2: Create src/components/EnergySlider.jsx ===

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { supabase } from '../lib/supabase'
import { getTodayIST } from '../lib/dateUtils'
import { Zap } from 'lucide-react'

const ENERGY_LABELS = {
  1: 'Drained', 2: 'Low', 3: 'Okay',
  4: 'Good', 5: 'Solid', 6: 'Focused',
  7: 'Sharp', 8: 'Energized', 9: 'Locked In', 10: 'Peak'
}

const ENERGY_COLORS = {
  low: '#C0392B',    // 1-3
  mid: '#E07B39',    // 4-6
  high: '#1A6B4A'    // 7-10
}

export default function EnergySlider() {
  const [energy, setEnergy] = useState(7)
  const [saved, setSaved] = useState(false)
  const [todayEnergy, setTodayEnergy] = useState(null)
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true)

  useEffect(() => {
    const load = async () => {
      const { data } = await supabase
        .from('ai_sessions')
        .select('user_input')
        .eq('type', 'energy_log')
        .eq('session_date', getTodayIST())
        .single()
      if (data?.user_input) {
        const val = parseInt(data.user_input)
        setTodayEnergy(val)
        setEnergy(val)
        setSaved(true)
      }
      setIsLoading(false)
    }
    load()
  }, [])

  const getColor = (val) => {
    if (val <= 3) return ENERGY_COLORS.low
    if (val <= 6) return ENERGY_COLORS.mid
    return ENERGY_COLORS.high
  }

  const save = async () => {
    const today = getTodayIST()
    const { data: existing } = await supabase
      .from('ai_sessions')
      .select('id')
      .eq('type', 'energy_log')
      .eq('session_date', today)
      .single()

    if (existing) {
      await supabase
        .from('ai_sessions')
        .update({ user_input: energy.toString() })
        .eq('id', existing.id)
    } else {
      await supabase.from('ai_sessions').insert({
        type: 'energy_log',
        session_date: today,
        user_input: energy.toString(),
        ai_response: '',
        context_snapshot: JSON.stringify({ 
          logged_at: new Date().toISOString() 
        })
      })
    }
    setTodayEnergy(energy)
    setSaved(true)
  }

  if (isLoading) return null

  return (
    <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-[#E5E0D8] p-5">
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <Zap size={14} style={{ color: getColor(energy) }}/>
          <p className="text-[10px] font-bold text-[#9A9590]
            font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-widest">
            Energy Level
          </p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <p className="text-lg font-bold font-['Space_Mono']"
            style={{ color: getColor(energy) }}>
            {energy}
          </p>
          <p className="text-xs text-[#9A9590] font-['Inter']">
            {ENERGY_LABELS[energy]}
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>

      <input
        type="range"
        min={1}
        max={10}
        value={energy}
        onChange={e => {
          setEnergy(parseInt(e.target.value))
          setSaved(false)
        }}
        className="w-full h-2 rounded-full appearance-none 
          cursor-pointer mb-3"
        style={{
          background: `linear-gradient(to right, 
            ${getColor(energy)} ${(energy - 1) / 9 * 100}%, 
            #E5E0D8 ${(energy - 1) / 9 * 100}%)`
        }}
      />

      <div className="flex justify-between text-[8px] 
        text-[#9A9590] font-['Space_Mono'] mb-3">
        <span>DRAINED</span>
        <span>PEAK</span>
      </div>

      {!saved ? (
        <button
          onClick={save}
          className="w-full py-2 rounded-xl text-xs font-bold
            font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-wider
            text-white transition-all"
          style={{ backgroundColor: getColor(energy) }}
        >
          Log Energy
        </button>
      ) : (
        <p className="text-center text-[10px] text-[#9A9590]
          font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-wider">
          ✓ Logged today — {ENERGY_LABELS[todayEnergy]}
        </p>
      )}
    </div>
  )
}

=== CHANGE 3: Create src/lib/correlationEngine.js ===

export async function getHabitCorrelations(supabase) {
  const thirtyDaysAgo = new Date()
  thirtyDaysAgo.setDate(thirtyDaysAgo.getDate() - 30)
  const fromDate = thirtyDaysAgo.toISOString().split('T')[0]

  const [energyRes, healthRes, questRes] = await Promise.all([
    supabase.from('ai_sessions')
      .select('session_date, user_input')
      .eq('type', 'energy_log')
      .gte('session_date', fromDate),
    supabase.from('health_logs')
      .select('log_date, sleep_done, day_score, gym_done')
      .gte('log_date', fromDate),
    supabase.from('daily_completions')
      .select('completed_date')
      .gte('completed_date', fromDate)
  ])

  const energyLogs = energyRes.data || []
  const healthLogs = healthRes.data || []
  const completions = questRes.data || []

  if (energyLogs.length < 7) return null

  const insights = []

  // Insight 1: Sleep vs Energy
  const sleepDays = healthLogs.filter(l => l.sleep_done)
  const noSleepDays = healthLogs.filter(l => !l.sleep_done)

  const avgEnergyWithSleep = sleepDays.reduce((sum, log) => {
    const e = energyLogs.find(e => e.session_date === log.log_date)
    return e ? sum + parseInt(e.user_input) : sum
  }, 0) / (sleepDays.length || 1)

  const avgEnergyWithoutSleep = noSleepDays.reduce((sum, log) => {
    const e = energyLogs.find(e => e.session_date === log.log_date)
    return e ? sum + parseInt(e.user_input) : sum
  }, 0) / (noSleepDays.length || 1)

  if (sleepDays.length >= 3 && noSleepDays.length >= 3) {
    const diff = Math.round(avgEnergyWithSleep - avgEnergyWithoutSleep)
    if (Math.abs(diff) >= 1) {
      insights.push({
        icon: '😴',
        text: `On good sleep days your energy is ${Math.abs(diff)} points ${diff > 0 ? 'higher' : 'lower'} on average`
      })
    }
  }

  // Insight 2: Gym vs Quest completion
  const gymDays = healthLogs
    .filter(l => l.gym_done)
    .map(l => l.log_date)
  
  const questsOnGymDays = completions
    .filter(c => gymDays.includes(c.completed_date)).length
  const questsOnNonGymDays = completions
    .filter(c => !gymDays.includes(c.completed_date)).length

  if (gymDays.length >= 3) {
    const gymRatio = questsOnGymDays / (gymDays.length || 1)
    const nonGymRatio = questsOnNonGymDays / 
      ((healthLogs.length - gymDays.length) || 1)
    const diff = Math.round((gymRatio - nonGymRatio) * 10) / 10
    if (Math.abs(diff) >= 0.5) {
      insights.push({
        icon: '🏋️',
        text: `On gym days you complete ${Math.abs(diff)} more quests on average`
      })
    }
  }

  // Insight 3: High energy vs health score
  const highEnergyDays = energyLogs
    .filter(e => parseInt(e.user_input) >= 7)
    .map(e => e.session_date)
  
  const healthOnHighEnergy = healthLogs
    .filter(l => highEnergyDays.includes(l.log_date))
    .reduce((sum, l) => sum + (l.day_score || 0), 0) / 
    (highEnergyDays.length || 1)

  const healthOnLowEnergy = healthLogs
    .filter(l => !highEnergyDays.includes(l.log_date))
    .reduce((sum, l) => sum + (l.day_score || 0), 0) / 
    ((healthLogs.length - highEnergyDays.length) || 1)

  if (highEnergyDays.length >= 3) {
    const diff = Math.round(healthOnHighEnergy - healthOnLowEnergy)
    if (Math.abs(diff) >= 10) {
      insights.push({
        icon: '⚡',
        text: `High energy days have ${Math.abs(diff)}% ${diff > 0 ? 'better' : 'worse'} health scores`
      })
    }
  }

  return insights.length > 0 ? insights : null
}

=== CHANGE 3: Add session performance stats ===

In TradingRoadmap.jsx, compute session stats from trades:

const sessionStats = useMemo(() => {
  const sessions = ['london', 'new_york', 'asian', 'overlap']
  return sessions.map(session => {
    const sessionTrades = trades.filter(t => t.session === session)
    if (sessionTrades.length === 0) return null
    const wins = sessionTrades.filter(t => parseFloat(t.pnl) > 0).length
    const winRate = Math.round((wins / sessionTrades.length) * 100)
    const totalPnl = sessionTrades
      .reduce((sum, t) => sum + parseFloat(t.pnl || 0), 0)
    return { 
      session, 
      trades: sessionTrades.length, 
      winRate, 
      totalPnl: Math.round(totalPnl * 100) / 100 
    }
  }).filter(Boolean)
}, [trades])

Add session stats section (below win rate / expectancy cards,
above trade calendar — only show if any trade has session data):

{sessionStats.length > 0 && (
  <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-[#E5E0D8] 
    p-5 mb-4">
    <p className="text-[10px] font-bold text-[#9A9590]
      font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-widest mb-3">
      Session Performance
    </p>
    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
      {sessionStats.map(stat => (
        <div key={stat.session}
          className="bg-[#F5F4F0] rounded-xl p-3">
          <p className="text-[9px] font-bold text-[#9A9590]
            font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-wider mb-1">
            {stat.session === 'new_york' ? 'New York'
              : stat.session === 'overlap' ? 'Overlap'
              : stat.session.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + 
                stat.session.slice(1)}
          </p>
          <p className="text-lg font-bold font-['Space_Mono']"
            style={{ 
              color: stat.winRate >= 50 ? '#1A6B4A' : '#C0392B' 
            }}>
            {stat.winRate}%
          </p>
          <p className="text-[9px] text-[#9A9590] 
            font-['Space_Mono']">
            {stat.trades} trades · {stat.totalPnl > 0 ? '+' : ''}{stat.totalPnl}
          </p>
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
    {sessionStats.length >= 2 && (
      <p className="text-[10px] text-[#E07B39] font-['Space_Mono']
        uppercase tracking-wider mt-3 font-bold">
        Best: {sessionStats.sort((a,b) => b.winRate - a.winRate)[0]
          .session.replace('_', ' ').toUpperCase()} session
      </p>
    )}
  </div>
)}

=== CHANGE 4: Add weekly trading letter ===

Add state to TradingRoadmap.jsx:
const [weeklyLetter, setWeeklyLetter] = useState(null)
const [isGeneratingLetter, setIsGeneratingLetter] = useState(false)
const [letterLoaded, setLetterLoaded] = useState(false)

Load saved letter on mount:
useEffect(() => {
  const loadLetter = async () => {
    const { data } = await supabase
      .from('ai_sessions')
      .select('ai_response, session_date')
      .eq('type', 'weekly_trading_letter')
      .order('session_date', { ascending: false })
      .limit(1)
      .single()
    if (data) setWeeklyLetter(data)
    setLetterLoaded(true)
  }
  loadLetter()
}, [])

Add letter generator:
const generateWeeklyLetter = async () => {
  setIsGeneratingLetter(true)
  try {
    const { callGroq } = await import('../lib/groq')

    const weekStart = new Date()
    weekStart.setDate(weekStart.getDate() - 7)
    const fromDate = weekStart.toISOString().split('T')[0]

    const { data: weekTrades } = await supabase
      .from('trades')
      .select('*')
      .gte('date', fromDate)

    const wins = (weekTrades || []).filter(t => 
      parseFloat(t.pnl) > 0).length
    const losses = (weekTrades || []).filter(t => 
      parseFloat(t.pnl) < 0).length
    const totalPnl = (weekTrades || [])
      .reduce((sum, t) => sum + parseFloat(t.pnl || 0), 0)
    const rulesViolations = (weekTrades || []).filter(t => 
      t.rules_followed === 'NO').length

    const result = await callGroq({
      messages: [{
        role: 'user',
        content: `Write a weekly trading performance letter 
        for Abhishek. He trades GBPUSD, EURUSD, XAUUSD 
        using ICT/SMC framework.
        
        This week:
        - Trades: ${weekTrades?.length || 0}
        - Wins: ${wins}, Losses: ${losses}
        - Total PnL: ${Math.round(totalPnl * 100) / 100}
        - Rules violations: ${rulesViolations}
        
        Write exactly 1 paragraph. Style: brutal honest 
        fund manager letter to himself. No fluff. 
        Reference specific numbers. End with one action 
        for next week. Max 120 words.`
      }],
      max_tokens: 300,
      temperature: 0.8
    })

    if (!result.error) {
      const today = getTodayIST()
      await supabase.from('ai_sessions').insert({
        type: 'weekly_trading_letter',
        session_date: today,
        ai_response: result.text,
        user_input: `trades:${weekTrades?.length}`,
        context_snapshot: JSON.stringify({ 
          wins, losses, totalPnl, rulesViolations 
        })
      })
      setWeeklyLetter({ 
        ai_response: result.text, 
        session_date: today 
      })
    }
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('letter error:', err)
  }
  setIsGeneratingLetter(false)
}

Add weekly letter card to TradingRoadmap
(below session performance, above trade log form):

{letterLoaded && (
  <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-[#E5E0D8] 
    p-5 mb-4">
    <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-3">
      <div>
        <p className="text-[10px] font-bold text-[#9A9590]
          font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-widest mb-0.5">
          Weekly Letter
        </p>
        <p className="text-sm font-bold text-[#1A1A2E] 
          font-['Inter']">
          JARVIS Verdict
        </p>
      </div>
      <button
        onClick={generateWeeklyLetter}
        disabled={isGeneratingLetter}
        className="bg-[#1A1A2E] text-white px-3 py-1.5 
          rounded-lg text-[9px] font-bold font-['Space_Mono']
          uppercase tracking-wider disabled:opacity-50"
      >
        {isGeneratingLetter ? 'Writing...' : 'Generate'}
      </button>
    </div>
    {weeklyLetter ? (
      <div className="bg-[#F5F4F0] rounded-xl p-4 
        border-l-4 border-[#1A1A2E]">
        <p className="text-sm text-[#1A1A2E] font-['Inter'] 
          leading-relaxed">
          {weeklyLetter.ai_response}
        </p>
        <p className="text-[9px] text-[#9A9590] 
          font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-wider mt-2">
          {weeklyLetter.session_date}
        </p>
      </div>
    ) : (
      <p className="text-xs text-[#9A9590] font-['Inter']">
        Generate your weekly trading assessment.
      </p>
    )}
  </div>
)}

PROMPT 7 — Cluster Completion Celebration
MISSION: Detect when all phase2 topics in a cluster are done.
Trigger a special celebration animation. Save milestone to
Supabase. Show completion badge on cluster cards.
Additive only — zero changes to togglePhase2 logic.

=== CHANGE 1: Add cluster completion detection to aiTrackStore.js ===

Add to initial state:
  completedClusters: {},
  clusterCompletionLoaded: false

Add loadCompletedClusters action:
loadCompletedClusters: async () => {
  const { data } = await supabase
    .from('ai_sessions')
    .select('context_snapshot, session_date')
    .eq('type', 'cluster_completion')
  
  const completed = {}
  ;(data || []).forEach(row => {
    try {
      const ctx = JSON.parse(row.context_snapshot)
      if (ctx.clusterId) {
        completed[ctx.clusterId] = {
          completedAt: row.session_date,
          topicsCompleted: ctx.topicsCompleted
        }
      }
    } catch {}
  })
  set({ completedClusters: completed, clusterCompletionLoaded: true })
},

Add checkClusterCompletion action:
checkClusterCompletion: async (clusterId, clusterName) => {
  const { progress, completedClusters } = get()

  // Already celebrated this cluster
  if (completedClusters[clusterId]) return

  // Get all topic IDs for this cluster
  const cluster = AI_TRACK_DATA.clusters.find(c => c.id === clusterId)
  if (!cluster) return

  const allTopicIds = cluster.sections.flatMap(s => 
    s.topics.map(t => t.id)
  )
  const completedCount = allTopicIds.filter(id => 
    progress[id]?.phase2_done
  ).length

  if (completedCount < allTopicIds.length) return

  // All topics done — save milestone
  const today = getTodayIST()
  await supabase.from('ai_sessions').insert({
    type: 'cluster_completion',
    session_date: today,
    user_input: clusterId,
    ai_response: clusterName,
    context_snapshot: JSON.stringify({
      clusterId,
      clusterName,
      topicsCompleted: allTopicIds.length,
      completedAt: new Date().toISOString()
    })
  })

  set(state => ({
    completedClusters: {
      ...state.completedClusters,
      [clusterId]: {
        completedAt: today,
        topicsCompleted: allTopicIds.length
      }
    }
  }))

  // Trigger celebration
  const { triggerClusterCelebration } = await import(
    '../components/ClusterCelebration'
  )
  triggerClusterCelebration(clusterName, allTopicIds.length)
},

Export: loadCompletedClusters, checkClusterCompletion, 
  completedClusters, clusterCompletionLoaded

Call loadCompletedClusters in AIEngineerTrack.jsx useEffect
alongside loadProgress and loadWeeklyGoals.

Call checkClusterCompletion in AIEngineerTrack.jsx after
every togglePhase2 call:

=== CHANGE 2: Create src/components/ClusterCelebration.jsx ===

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react'
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion'
import { Trophy } from 'lucide-react'

let celebrationCallback = null

export function triggerClusterCelebration(clusterName, topicCount) {
  if (celebrationCallback) {
    celebrationCallback(clusterName, topicCount)
  }
}

const CLUSTER_COLORS = {
  'A': '#E07B39',
  'B': '#1A6B4A', 
  'C': '#7C3AED'
}

export default function ClusterCelebration() {
  const [celebration, setCelebration] = useState(null)

  useEffect(() => {
    celebrationCallback = (clusterName, topicCount) => {
      setCelebration({ clusterName, topicCount })
    }
    return () => { celebrationCallback = null }
  }, [])

  if (!celebration) return null

  // Detect cluster letter from name
  const clusterLetter = Object.keys(CLUSTER_COLORS).find(k => 
    celebration.clusterName.includes(k)
  ) || 'A'
  const color = CLUSTER_COLORS[clusterLetter]

  return (
    <AnimatePresence>
      {celebration && (
        <motion.div
          initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
          exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
          className="fixed inset-0 z-[200] flex items-center 
            justify-center"
          style={{ backgroundColor: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.85)' }}
          onClick={() => setCelebration(null)}
        >
          {/* Particle burst */}
          {[...Array(16)].map((_, i) => (
            <motion.div
              key={i}
              className="absolute w-2 h-2 rounded-full"
              style={{ backgroundColor: color }}
              initial={{ x: 0, y: 0, opacity: 1 }}
              animate={{
                x: Math.cos((i / 16) * Math.PI * 2) * 
                  (120 + Math.random() * 80),
                y: Math.sin((i / 16) * Math.PI * 2) * 
                  (120 + Math.random() * 80),
                opacity: 0,
                scale: [1, 1.5, 0]
              }}
              transition={{ 
                duration: 1.2, 
                delay: 0.2,
                ease: 'easeOut' 
              }}
            />
          ))}

          <motion.div
            initial={{ scale: 0.5, opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
            animate={{ scale: 1, opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
            transition={{ type: 'spring', bounce: 0.4, delay: 0.1 }}
            className="text-center px-8 py-10 rounded-3xl 
              border-2 max-w-sm w-full mx-4"
            style={{ 
              backgroundColor: '#1A1A2E',
              borderColor: color 
            }}
            onClick={e => e.stopPropagation()}
          >
            <motion.div
              animate={{ rotate: [0, -10, 10, -10, 10, 0] }}
              transition={{ delay: 0.5, duration: 0.6 }}
              className="w-16 h-16 rounded-2xl flex items-center 
                justify-center mx-auto mb-4"
              style={{ backgroundColor: color }}
            >
              <Trophy size={32} className="text-white"/>
            </motion.div>

            <p className="text-[10px] font-bold text-white/50
              font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-widest mb-2">
              Cluster Complete
            </p>
            <p className="text-2xl font-bold text-white 
              font-['Inter'] mb-1">
              {celebration.clusterName}
            </p>
            <p className="text-sm text-white/60 font-['Inter'] mb-6">
              {celebration.topicCount} topics mastered
            </p>

            <motion.div
              initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
              transition={{ delay: 0.8 }}
              className="bg-white/5 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 mb-6
                border border-white/10"
            >
              <p className="text-xs text-white/70 font-['Inter']">
                This cluster is locked in. The knowledge compounds 
                from here.
              </p>
            </motion.div>

            <button
              onClick={() => setCelebration(null)}
              className="w-full py-3 rounded-xl text-sm font-bold
                font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-wider
                text-white transition-all"
              style={{ backgroundColor: color }}
            >
              Continue
            </button>
          </motion.div>
        </motion.div>
      )}
    </AnimatePresence>
  )
}

generateQuiz: async (concept) => {
  try {
    const { callGroq } = await import('../lib/groq')
    const result = await callGroq({
      messages: [{
        role: 'user',
        content: `Generate exactly 2 retention questions for 
        this concept: "${concept.title}"
        Context: ${concept.description || concept.title}
        
        Return ONLY valid JSON array, no markdown:
        [
          {
            "question": "...",
            "options": ["A: ...", "B: ...", "C: ...", "D: ..."],
            "correct": 0,
            "explanation": "..."
          },
          {
            "question": "...",
            "options": ["A: ...", "B: ...", "C: ...", "D: ..."],
            "correct": 2,
            "explanation": "..."
          }
        ]`
      }],
      max_tokens: 500,
      temperature: 0.6
    })

    if (!result.error) {
      const clean = result.text
        .replace(/```json|```/g, '').trim()
      const questions = JSON.parse(clean)
      set({ 
        activeQuiz: { 
          concept: concept.title,
          questions,
          currentQ: 0,
          score: 0,
          done: false
        }
      })
    }
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('quiz gen error:', err)
  }
},

Add answerQuiz action:
answerQuiz: (answerIndex) => {
  const { activeQuiz } = get()
  if (!activeQuiz) return
  
  const isCorrect = answerIndex === 
    activeQuiz.questions[activeQuiz.currentQ].correct
  const newScore = activeQuiz.score + (isCorrect ? 1 : 0)
  const isLast = activeQuiz.currentQ === 
    activeQuiz.questions.length - 1

  if (isLast) {
    set({ 
      activeQuiz: { 
        ...activeQuiz, 
        score: newScore, 
        done: true,
        lastAnswer: answerIndex
      },
      quizHistory: {
        ...get().quizHistory,
        [activeQuiz.concept]: { 
          score: newScore, 
          total: activeQuiz.questions.length,
          date: new Date().toISOString()
        }
      }
    })
  } else {
    set({
      activeQuiz: {
        ...activeQuiz,
        score: newScore,
        currentQ: activeQuiz.currentQ + 1,
        lastAnswer: answerIndex
      }
    })
  }
},

dismissQuiz: () => set({ activeQuiz: null }),

generateConnections: async () => {
  const { topicArchive } = get()
  if (!topicArchive || topicArchive.length < 3) return
  
  set({ isGeneratingConnections: true })
  
  try {
    const { callGroq } = await import('../lib/groq')
    const topicTitles = topicArchive
      .slice(0, 8)
      .map(t => t.topic_data?.title || t.domain)
      .join(', ')

    const result = await callGroq({
      messages: [{
        role: 'user',
        content: `These are Abhishek's recent study topics:
        ${topicTitles}
        
        Find 3 non-obvious intellectual connections between 
        these topics. Each connection must reference exactly 
        2 of the topics listed.
        
        Return ONLY valid JSON, no markdown:
        [
          {
            "topic1": "...",
            "topic2": "...",
            "connection": "One sentence explaining the link",
            "insight": "Why this matters for an AI engineer"
          }
        ]`
      }],
      max_tokens: 400,
      temperature: 0.8
    })

    if (!result.error) {
      const clean = result.text
        .replace(/```json|```/g, '').trim()
      const connections = JSON.parse(clean)
      set({ topicConnections: connections })
    }
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('connections error:', err)
  }
  set({ isGeneratingConnections: false })
},

updateConceptStreak: async () => {
  const today = getTodayIST()
  const { lastConceptDate, conceptStreak } = get()
  
  if (lastConceptDate === today) return // already counted today
  
  const yesterday = new Date()
  yesterday.setDate(yesterday.getDate() - 1)
  const yesterdayStr = yesterday.toISOString().split('T')[0]
  
  const newStreak = lastConceptDate === yesterdayStr 
    ? conceptStreak + 1 
    : 1
  
  set({ conceptStreak: newStreak, lastConceptDate: today })
  
  await supabase
    .from('knowledge_depth')
    .upsert({ 
      domain: '_streak',
      brain_drops: newStreak,
      topics_explored: newStreak
    }, { onConflict: 'domain' })

  if (newStreak % 7 === 0) {
    triggerJarvisToast({
      type: 'success',
      title: `${newStreak} Day Explorer Streak`,
      message: 'Reading daily. Knowledge compounds.',
      xp: 25
    })
  }
},

=== CHANGE 1: Add completion rate tracking to questStore.js ===

Add to initial state:
  weeklyCompletionRate: 0,
  domainCompletionMap: {}

Add computeWeeklyStats action:
computeWeeklyStats: async () => {
  const weekStart = new Date()
  weekStart.setDate(weekStart.getDate() - 7)
  const fromDate = weekStart.toISOString().split('T')[0]

  const [completionsRes, questsRes] = await Promise.all([
    supabase.from('daily_completions')
      .select('quest_id, completed_date')
      .gte('completed_date', fromDate),
    supabase.from('daily_quests')
      .select('id, domain, difficulty')
      .eq('is_active', true)
  ])

  const completions = completionsRes.data || []
  const quests = questsRes.data || []
  
  const completedIds = new Set(completions.map(c => c.quest_id))
  const completionRate = quests.length > 0
    ? Math.round((completedIds.size / quests.length) * 100)
    : 0

  // Domain completion map
  const domainMap = {}
  const domains = ['sde', 'trading', 'health', 'explorer', 
    'ai_track', 'finance']
  
  domains.forEach(domain => {
    const domainQuests = quests.filter(q => q.domain === domain)
    const domainDone = domainQuests
      .filter(q => completedIds.has(q.id)).length
    domainMap[domain] = {
      total: domainQuests.length,
      completed: domainDone,
      rate: domainQuests.length > 0
        ? Math.round((domainDone / domainQuests.length) * 100)
        : null,
      lastCompletionDate: completions
        .filter(c => {
          const q = quests.find(q => q.id === c.quest_id)
          return q?.domain === domain
        })
        .sort((a,b) => 
          new Date(b.completed_date) - new Date(a.completed_date)
        )[0]?.completed_date || null
    }
  })

  set({ 
    weeklyCompletionRate: completionRate,
    domainCompletionMap: domainMap
  })
},

Export: computeWeeklyStats, weeklyCompletionRate, 
  domainCompletionMap

Call computeWeeklyStats in loadQuests action
(at the end, after existing load logic).

=== CHANGE 3: Add domain imbalance detection ===

Create src/lib/domainBalancer.js:

const DOMAIN_LABELS = {
  sde: 'SDE / DSA',
  trading: 'Trading',
  health: 'Health',
  explorer: 'Explorer',
  ai_track: 'AI Track',
  finance: 'Finance'
}

const DOMAIN_ICONS = {
  sde: '💻',
  trading: '📈',
  health: '💪',
  explorer: '🧠',
  ai_track: '🤖',
  finance: '📚'
}

export function detectDomainImbalance(domainCompletionMap) {
  const alerts = []
  const today = new Date()

  Object.entries(domainCompletionMap).forEach(([domain, data]) => {
    if (data.total === 0) return // no quests in domain
    
    // Check last completion date
    if (data.lastCompletionDate) {
      const lastDate = new Date(data.lastCompletionDate)
      const daysSince = Math.floor(
        (today - lastDate) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24)
      )
      
      if (daysSince >= 5) {
        alerts.push({
          domain,
          label: DOMAIN_LABELS[domain],
          icon: DOMAIN_ICONS[domain],
          message: `No ${DOMAIN_LABELS[domain]} quests in ${daysSince} days`,
          severity: daysSince >= 10 ? 'high' : 'medium'
        })
      }
    } else if (data.total > 0) {
      // Quests exist but none ever completed
      alerts.push({
        domain,
        label: DOMAIN_LABELS[domain],
        icon: DOMAIN_ICONS[domain],
        message: `${DOMAIN_LABELS[domain]} quests never attempted`,
        severity: 'low'
      })
    }
  })

  // Sort by severity
  const severityOrder = { high: 0, medium: 1, low: 2 }
  return alerts
    .sort((a,b) => severityOrder[a.severity] - severityOrder[b.severity])
    .slice(0, 2) // max 2 alerts shown
}

  [domainCompletionMap]

  <div className="bg-white rounded-2xl border border-[#E5E0D8] 
    p-4 mb-4">

          {alert.message}
        </p>

          font-['Space_Mono'] uppercase tracking-wider
          ${alert.severity === 'high' 
            ? 'text-[#C0392B]' 
            : 'text-[#E07B39]'}`}>
          {alert.severity}

    ))}

)}

PROMPT 10 — Time Logged Per AI Track Topic
